#### Opcodes

```
  0: 0x0005 [0x9D] Remap Work_Zone[6*] -> EventData[0x0018]
  1: 0x000B [0x9D] Remap Work_Zone[7*] -> EventData[0x0E78]
  2: 0x0011 [0x9D] Remap Work_Zone[8*] -> EventData[0x1CD8]
  3: 0x0017 [0x00] END_REQSTACK()
```
